    SELECT [j0].[JobUserTaskId], [j0].[JobId], [j0].[UserId], [j0].[TaskId], [t].[TaskId] AS [TaskId0], [t].[CompletedDate], [t].[CreatedAt], [t].[Description], [t].[DueDate], [t].[Notes], [t].[Priority], [t].[Status], [t].[Title], [t].[UpdatedAt], [a].[Id], [a].[AccessFailedCount], [a].[ConcurrencyStamp], [a].[DOB], [a].[Email], [a].[EmailConfirmed], [a].[FirstName], [a].[HireDate], [a].[IsActive], [a].[LastName], [a].[LockoutEnabled], [a].[LockoutEnd], [a].[MiddleName], [a].[NormalizedEmail], [a].[NormalizedUserName], [a].[PasswordHash], [a].[PhoneNumber], [a].[PhoneNumberConfirmed], [a].[SecurityStamp], [a].[TwoFactorEnabled], [a].[UserName]
    FROM [JobUserTasks] AS [j0]
    INNER JOIN [Tasks] AS [t] ON [j0].[TaskId] = [t].[TaskId]
    INNER JOIN [AspNetUsers] AS [a] ON [j0].[UserId] = [a].[Id]
) AS [t0] ON [j].[JobId] = [t0].[JobId]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [j1].[JobUserNoteId], [j1].[JobId], [j1].[UserId], [j1].[NoteId], [n].[NoteId] AS [NoteId0], [n].[CreatedAt], [n].[Note], [a0].[Id], [a0].[AccessFailedCount], [a0].[ConcurrencyStamp], [a0].[DOB], [a0].[Email], [a0].[EmailConfirmed], [a0].[FirstName], [a0].[HireDate], [a0].[IsActive], [a0].[LastName], [a0].[LockoutEnabled], [a0].[LockoutEnd], [a0].[MiddleName], [a0].[NormalizedEmail], [a0].[NormalizedUserName], [a0].[PasswordHash], [a0].[PhoneNumber], [a0].[PhoneNumberConfirmed], [a0].[SecurityStamp], [a0].[TwoFactorEnabled], [a0].[UserName]
    FROM [JobUserNotes] AS [j1]
    INNER JOIN [Notes] AS [n] ON [j1].[NoteId] = [n].[NoteId]
    INNER JOIN [AspNetUsers] AS [a0] ON [j1].[UserId] = [a0].[Id]
) AS [t1] ON [j].[JobId] = [t1].[JobId]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [c].[JobId], [c].[CustomerId], [c].[CustomerJobsId], [c0].[CustomerId] AS [CustomerId0], [c0].[Address], [c0].[City], [c0].[ContactPerson], [c0].[CustomerType], [c0].[Email], [c0].[Fax], [c0].[Industry], [c0].[Name], [c0].[Notes], [c0].[Phone], [c0].[State], [c0].[Status], [c0].[Website], [c0].[ZipCode]
    FROM [CustomerJobs] AS [c]
    INNER JOIN [Customers] AS [c0] ON [c].[CustomerId] = [c0].[CustomerId]
) AS [t2] ON [j].[JobId] = [t2].[JobId]
ORDER BY [j].[JobId], [t0].[JobUserTaskId], [t0].[JobId], [t0].[UserId], [t0].[TaskId], [t0].[TaskId0], [t0].[Id], [t1].[JobUserNoteId], [t1].[JobId], [t1].[UserId], [t1].[NoteId], [t1].[NoteId0], [t1].[Id], [t2].[JobId], [t2].[CustomerId], [t2].[CustomerJobsId]
